namespace = bccheatmenu
@MinPopCountrySelect = 1	#The minimal amount of pops required to be shown on the 'Select Empire' screen 


### Preparation ###
country_event = {
	id = bccheatmenu.999
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	trigger = {
		not = { has_country_flag = bc_is_in_menu }
	}
	after = {
		country_event = {
			id = bccheatmenu.1000
		}
	}
}

### BetterCheats Introduction Screen ###
country_event = {
	id = bccheatmenu.1000
	title = "bccheatmenu_1000_title"
	desc = "bccheatmenu_1000_desc"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
	}
	picture_event_data = {
		room = extradimensional_blue_room
	}
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = bc_is_in_menu
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				num_pops = 0
			}
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_1 
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_2 
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_3 
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_4 
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_5 
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_6 
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_7 
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_8 
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_9 
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_10
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_11
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_12
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_13
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_14
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_15
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_16
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_17
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_18
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_19
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_20
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_21
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_22
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_23
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_24
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_25
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_26
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_27
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_28
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_29
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_30
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_31
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_32
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_33
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_34
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_35
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_36
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_37
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_38
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_39
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_40
		}
	}

	# Allow Player to Cheat #
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_1000_option_1"
		allow = {
			is_multiplayer = yes
			has_country_flag = bc_hosting
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = BetterCheats_granting_access
			set_country_flag = BetterCheats_selecting_player
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.1
			}
		}
	}

	# Your Own Cheats #
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_1000_option_2"
		allow = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = bc_allow_cheating_self
				has_country_flag = bc_hosting
				is_multiplayer = no
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_selected
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.2
			}
		}
	}

	# Other Player Cheats #
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_1000_option_3"
		allow = {
			OR = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = bc_allow_cheating_other
					has_country_flag = bc_allow_cheating_self
				}
				has_country_flag = bc_hosting
			}
			is_multiplayer = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = BetterCheats_selecting_player
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.1
			}
		}
	}

	# AI Cheats #
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_1000_option_4"
		allow = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = bc_allow_cheating_other
				has_country_flag = bc_hosting
				is_multiplayer = no
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = BetterCheats_selecting_ai
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.1
			}
		}
	}

	# Special Event #
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_1000_option_5"
		allow = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = bc_hosting
				is_multiplayer = no
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.5
			}
		}
	}

	# Close # 
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_close"
		default_hide_option = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_country_flag = bc_is_in_menu
		}
	}
	
}

### Empire Selection ###
country_event = {
	id = bccheatmenu.1
	title = "bccheatmenu_1_title"
	desc = "bccheatmenu_1_desc"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
	}
	picture_event_data = {
		room = extradimensional_blue_room
	}
	after = {
		remove_country_flag = BetterCheats_selecting_player
		remove_country_flag = BetterCheats_selecting_ai
		remove_country_flag = BetterCheats_granting_access
	}
	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						PREV = { has_country_flag = BetterCheats_selecting_ai }
						is_primitive = no
						num_pops > @MinPopCountrySelect
						is_ai = yes
					}
					AND = {
						PREV = { PREV = { has_country_flag = BetterCheats_selecting_player } }
						is_ai = no
						num_pops > @MinPopCountrySelect
					}

				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_1
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						PREV = { has_country_flag = BetterCheats_selecting_ai }
						is_primitive = no
						num_pops > @MinPopCountrySelect
						is_ai = yes
					}
					AND = {
						PREV = { has_country_flag = BetterCheats_selecting_player }
						is_ai = no
						num_pops > @MinPopCountrySelect
					}

				}

				NOT = { is_same_value = event_target:cheat_target_1 }
			}
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_2
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						PREV = { has_country_flag = BetterCheats_selecting_ai }
						is_primitive = no
						num_pops > @MinPopCountrySelect
						is_ai = yes

						PREV = { has_country_flag = BetterCheats_selecting_player }

						num_pops > @MinPopCountrySelect
					}

				}
				NOT = { is_same_value = event_target:cheat_target_1 }
				NOT = { is_same_value = event_target:cheat_target_2 }
			}
			save_event_target_as = cheat_target_3
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {

	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_cheat_target_aa"
		trigger = {
		event_target:cheat_target_1 = { 
			exists = this
			num_pops > @MinPopCountrySelect
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:cheat_target_1 = { save_event_target_as = cheat_target_selected }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = BetterCheats_granting_access
					}
				country_event = {
					id = bccheatmenu.10
					}
				}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = bccheatmenu.2
				}
			}
		}
	}

### Grand Access to Cheats ###
country_event = {
	id = bccheatmenu.10
	title = "bccheatmenu_10_title"
	desc = "bccheatmenu_10_desc"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
	}
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		planet_background = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		graphical_culture = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		city_level = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		room = event_target:cheat_target_selected.ruler
	}
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_10_option_1"
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				set_country_flag = bc_allow_cheating_self
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.10
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				set_country_flag = bc_inform_permission_updated
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			nand = {
				event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
					has_country_flag = bc_allow_cheating_self
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_10_option_1_1"
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				remove_country_flag = bc_allow_cheating_self
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.10
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				set_country_flag = bc_inform_permission_updated
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			and = {
				event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
					has_country_flag = bc_allow_cheating_self
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_10_option_2"
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				set_country_flag = bc_allow_cheating_other
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.10
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				set_country_flag = bc_inform_permission_updated
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			nand = {
				event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
					has_country_flag = bc_allow_cheating_other
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_10_option_2_1"
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				remove_country_flag = bc_allow_cheating_other
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.10
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				set_country_flag = bc_inform_permission_updated
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			and = {
				event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
					has_country_flag = bc_allow_cheating_other
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_10_option_3"
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				set_country_flag = bc_allow_planet_colonized
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.10
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				set_country_flag = bc_inform_permission_updated
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			nand = {
				event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
					has_country_flag = bc_allow_planet_colonized
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_10_option_3_1"
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				remove_country_flag = bc_allow_planet_colonized
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.10
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				set_country_flag = bc_inform_permission_updated

					has_country_flag = bc_allow_planet_colonized
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {

			}

	}

		name = "bccheatmenu_back"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.1000
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				country_event = {
					id = bcmultiplayer.3
				}
			}

		}
		default_hide_option = yes
	}

country_event = {
	id = bccheatmenu.2
	title = "bccheatmenu_2_title"
	desc = "bccheatmenu_2_desc"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
	}

		portrait = event_target:cheat_target_selected

		city_level = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		room = event_target:cheat_target_selected.ruler
	}
	#### EXAMPLE TIER BUTTON START ####
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_100_title"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.100
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			always = no # DELETE #
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				nor = {
					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t1
					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t2
					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t3
					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t4
					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t5
					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t6
					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t7
					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t8
					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t9
					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t10

			}
		}

				id = bccheatmenu.100
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			always = no # DELETE #

				or = {
					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t1
					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t2

					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t6
					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t7

			}

### Special Category ###
country_event = {
	id = bccheatmenu.57
	title = "bccheatmenu_57_title"
	desc = "bccheatmenu_57_desc"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		planet_background = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		graphical_culture = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		city_level = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		room = event_target:cheat_target_selected.ruler
	}

	### Explore ###
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_57_option_1"
		custom_tooltip  = "bccheatmenu_57_option_1_desc"
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				create_fleet = {
					name = "NAME_Other_Science_Ship"
					effect = {
						set_owner = prev
						create_ship_design = {
							design = "NAME_Prototype"
						}
						create_ship = {
							name = "NAME_From_Beyond"
							design = last_created_design
							graphical_culture = "extra_dimensional_01"
							prefix = no
							upgradable = no
						}
						set_location = starbase
					}
				}
				######## currently not working
				########every_system = {
				########	last_created_ship = {
				########		set_location = PREV
				########	}
				########}
			}
			destroy_ship = last_created_ship
			destroy_fleet = last_created_fleet
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.57
			}
		}
	}

	### Communications ###
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_57_option_3"
		custom_tooltip  = "bccheatmenu_57_option_3_desc"
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				every_country = {
					establish_communications_no_message = event_target:cheat_target_selected
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.57
			}
		}
	}

	# Back # 
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_back"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.2
			}
		}
		default_hide_option = yes
	}
	
}

#### EXAMPLE TIER SELECTOR ####
country_event = {
	id = bccheatmenu.100
	title = "bccheatmenu_100_title"
	desc = "bccheatmenu_100_desc"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
	}
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		planet_background = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		graphical_culture = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		city_level = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		room = event_target:cheat_target_selected.ruler
	}
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_disable"
		allow = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				or = {
					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t1
					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t2
					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t3
					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t4
					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t5
					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t6
					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t7
					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t8
					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t9
					has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t10
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
			remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t1
			remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t2
			remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t3
			remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t4
			remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t5
			remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t6
			remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t7
			remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t8
			remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t9
			remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.100
			}
		}

	}
	option = {
		name = "bc_tier_i"
		custom_tooltip = "bccheatmenu_100_t1_desc"
		allow = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				not = { has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t1 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.100
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t1
				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t2
				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t3
				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t4
				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t5
				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t6
				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t7
				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t8
				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t9
				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t10
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t1
					days = -1
				}
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t1
				days = -1
			}
		}
		
	}
	option = {
		name = "bc_tier_ii"
		custom_tooltip = "bccheatmenu_100_t2_desc"
		allow = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				not = { has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t2 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.100
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t1
				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t2
				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t3
				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t4
				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t5
				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t6
				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t7
				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t8
				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t9
				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t10
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t2
					days = -1
				}
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t2
				days = -1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "bc_tier_iii"
		custom_tooltip = "bccheatmenu_100_t3_desc"
		allow = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				not = { has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t3 }

		}
		hidden_effect = {

			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t1

				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t6
				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE_t7

#### EXAMPLE2 BOOL SELECTOR ####
country_event = {
	id = bccheatmenu.101
	title = "bccheatmenu_101_title"
	desc = "bccheatmenu_101_desc"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
	}
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		planet_background = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		graphical_culture = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		city_level = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		room = event_target:cheat_target_selected.ruler
	}
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_activate"
		custom_tooltip = "bccheatmenu_101_activate_desc"
		allow = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				not = { has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE2 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.101
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = bc_EXAMPLE2
					days = -1
				}
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = bc_EXAMPLE2
				days = -1
			}
		}
		
	}
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_deactivate"
		custom_tooltip = "bccheatmenu_101_deactivate_desc"
		allow = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				has_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE2
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.101
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE2
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			remove_modifier = bc_EXAMPLE2
		}
		
	}

	# Back #

		name = "bccheatmenu_back"

			}

	desc = "bccheatmenu_102_desc"

		is_ai = no

		planet_background = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		graphical_culture = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		city_level = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		room = event_target:cheat_target_selected.ruler
	}
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_disable"
		allow = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				or = {
					has_modifier = bc_energy_t1
					has_modifier = bc_energy_t2
					has_modifier = bc_energy_t3
					has_modifier = bc_energy_t4
					has_modifier = bc_energy_t5
					has_modifier = bc_energy_t6
					has_modifier = bc_energy_t7
					has_modifier = bc_energy_t8
					has_modifier = bc_energy_t9
					has_modifier = bc_energy_t10
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
			remove_modifier = bc_energy_t1
			remove_modifier = bc_energy_t2
			remove_modifier = bc_energy_t3
			remove_modifier = bc_energy_t4
			remove_modifier = bc_energy_t5
			remove_modifier = bc_energy_t6
			remove_modifier = bc_energy_t7
			remove_modifier = bc_energy_t8
			remove_modifier = bc_energy_t9
			remove_modifier = bc_energy_t10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.102
			}
		}

	}

		name = "bc_tier_i"

#### resource_cap BOOL SELECTOR ####
country_event = {
	id = bccheatmenu.110
	title = "bccheatmenu_110_title"
	desc = "bccheatmenu_110_desc"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
	}
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		planet_background = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		graphical_culture = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		city_level = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		room = event_target:cheat_target_selected.ruler
	}
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_activate"
		custom_tooltip = "bccheatmenu_110_activate_desc"
		allow = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				not = { has_modifier = bc_resource_cap }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.110
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = bc_resource_cap
					days = -1
				}
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = bc_resource_cap
				days = -1
			}
		}
		
	}
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_deactivate"
		custom_tooltip = "bccheatmenu_110_deactivate_desc"
		allow = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				has_modifier = bc_resource_cap
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.110
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				remove_modifier = bc_resource_cap
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			remove_modifier = bc_resource_cap
		}
		
	}

	# Back # 
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_back"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.50
			}
		}
		default_hide_option = yes
	}
}

#### monthly_loyalty | monthly_loyalty_from_subjects TIER SELECTOR ####
country_event = {
	id = bccheatmenu.1156
	title = "bccheatmenu_1156_title"
	desc = "bccheatmenu_1156_desc"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
	}
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		planet_background = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		graphical_culture = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		city_level = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		room = event_target:cheat_target_selected.ruler
	}
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_disable"
		allow = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				or = {
					has_modifier = bc_monthly_loyalty_t1
					has_modifier = bc_monthly_loyalty_t2
					has_modifier = bc_monthly_loyalty_t3
					has_modifier = bc_monthly_loyalty_t4

					has_modifier = bc_monthly_loyalty_t8

				}
			}
		}

			remove_modifier = bc_monthly_loyalty_t1
			remove_modifier = bc_monthly_loyalty_t2
			remove_modifier = bc_monthly_loyalty_t3

			remove_modifier = bc_monthly_loyalty_t5

				id = bccheatmenu.1156

#### diplomacy BOOL SELECTOR ####
country_event = {
	id = bccheatmenu.116
	title = "bccheatmenu_116_title"
	desc = "bccheatmenu_116_desc"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
	}
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		planet_background = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		graphical_culture = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		city_level = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		room = event_target:cheat_target_selected.ruler
	}
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_activate"
		custom_tooltip = "bccheatmenu_116_activate_desc"
		allow = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				not = { has_modifier = bc_diplomacy }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.116
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = bc_diplomacy
					days = -1
				}
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = bc_diplomacy
				days = -1
			}
		}
		
	}
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_deactivate"
		custom_tooltip = "bccheatmenu_116_deactivate_desc"
		allow = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				has_modifier = bc_diplomacy
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.116
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				remove_modifier = bc_diplomacy
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			remove_modifier = bc_diplomacy
		}
		
	}

	# Back # 
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_back"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.51
			}
		}
		default_hide_option = yes
	}
}

#### tech_alt BOOL SELECTOR ####
country_event = {
	id = bccheatmenu.121
	title = "bccheatmenu_121_title"
	desc = "bccheatmenu_121_desc"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
	}
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		planet_background = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		graphical_culture = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		city_level = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		room = event_target:cheat_target_selected.ruler
	}
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_activate"
		custom_tooltip = "bccheatmenu_121_activate_desc"
		allow = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				not = { has_modifier = bc_tech_alt }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.121
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = bc_tech_alt
					days = -1
				}
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = bc_tech_alt
				days = -1
			}
		}
		
	}
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_deactivate"
		custom_tooltip = "bccheatmenu_121_deactivate_desc"
		allow = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				has_modifier = bc_tech_alt
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.121
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				remove_modifier = bc_tech_alt
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			remove_modifier = bc_tech_alt
		}
		
	}

	# Back # 
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_back"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.55
			}
		}
		default_hide_option = yes
	}

#### anomaly_gen BOOL SELECTOR ####
country_event = {
	id = bccheatmenu.123
	title = "bccheatmenu_123_title"
	desc = "bccheatmenu_123_desc"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
	}
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		planet_background = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		graphical_culture = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		city_level = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		room = event_target:cheat_target_selected.ruler
	}
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_activate"
		custom_tooltip = "bccheatmenu_123_activate_desc"
		allow = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				not = { has_modifier = bc_anomaly_gen }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.123
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = bc_anomaly_gen
					days = -1
				}
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = bc_anomaly_gen
				days = -1
			}
		}
		
	}
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_deactivate"
		custom_tooltip = "bccheatmenu_123_deactivate_desc"
		allow = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				has_modifier = bc_anomaly_gen
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.123
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				remove_modifier = bc_anomaly_gen
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			remove_modifier = bc_anomaly_gen
		}
		
	}

	# Back # 
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_back"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.55
			}
		}
		default_hide_option = yes
	}
}

		is_ai = no

				}
			}
		}

	diplomatic = yes

		is_ai = no
	}
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		planet_background = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		graphical_culture = event_target:cheat_target_selected

		room = event_target:cheat_target_selected.ruler
	}

		name = "bccheatmenu_disable"

			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				or = {
					has_modifier = bc_happiness_t1

					has_modifier = bc_happiness_t3
					has_modifier = bc_happiness_t4

					has_modifier = bc_happiness_t7

country_event = {
	id = bccheatmenu.134
	title = "bccheatmenu_134_title"
	desc = "bccheatmenu_134_desc"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
	}
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		planet_background = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		graphical_culture = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		city_level = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		room = event_target:cheat_target_selected.ruler
	}
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_activate"
		custom_tooltip = "bccheatmenu_134_activate_desc"
		allow = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				not = { has_modifier = bc_ethics_shift }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.134
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = bc_ethics_shift
					days = -1
				}
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = bc_ethics_shift
				days = -1
			}
		}
		
	}
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_deactivate"
		custom_tooltip = "bccheatmenu_134_deactivate_desc"
		allow = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				has_modifier = bc_ethics_shift
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.134
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				remove_modifier = bc_ethics_shift
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			remove_modifier = bc_ethics_shift
		}
		
	}

	# Back # 
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_back"

			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.51
			}

#### leader_level BOOL SELECTOR ####
country_event = {
	id = bccheatmenu.136
	title = "bccheatmenu_136_title"
	desc = "bccheatmenu_136_desc"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
	}
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		planet_background = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		graphical_culture = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		city_level = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		room = event_target:cheat_target_selected.ruler
	}
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_activate"
		custom_tooltip = "bccheatmenu_136_activate_desc"
		allow = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				not = { has_modifier = bc_leader_level }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.136
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = bc_leader_level
					days = -1
				}
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = bc_leader_level
				days = -1
			}
		}
		
	}
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_deactivate"
		custom_tooltip = "bccheatmenu_136_deactivate_desc"
		allow = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				has_modifier = bc_leader_level
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.136
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				remove_modifier = bc_leader_level
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			remove_modifier = bc_leader_level
		}
		
	}

	# Back # 
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_back"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.54
			}
		}
		default_hide_option = yes
	}
}

#### ship_xp BOOL SELECTOR ####
country_event = {
	id = bccheatmenu.139
	title = "bccheatmenu_139_title"
	desc = "bccheatmenu_139_desc"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
	}
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		planet_background = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		graphical_culture = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		city_level = event_target:cheat_target_selected
		room = event_target:cheat_target_selected.ruler
	}
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_activate"
		custom_tooltip = "bccheatmenu_139_activate_desc"
		allow = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				not = { has_modifier = bc_ship_xp }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.139
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = bc_ship_xp
					days = -1
				}
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = bc_ship_xp
				days = -1
			}
		}
		
	}
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_deactivate"
		custom_tooltip = "bccheatmenu_139_deactivate_desc"
		allow = {
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				has_modifier = bc_ship_xp
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.139
			}
			event_target:cheat_target_selected = {
				remove_modifier = bc_ship_xp
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			remove_modifier = bc_ship_xp
		}
		
	}

	# Back # 
	option = {
		name = "bccheatmenu_back"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bccheatmenu.52
			}
		}
		default_hide_option = yes
	}
}
